  • /sample/Vector
    "import
        ion.*

    export
        class Vector
            var x: Number
            var y: Number
            var z: Number

            # obviously this is more concise and readable
            let length = (x * x + y * y + z * z) ^ 0.5

        # let length = (v: Vector) => (v.x * v.x + v.y * v.y + v.z * v.z) ^ 0.5
        # let scale = (v: Vector, s: Number) => Vector(v.x * s, v.y * s, v.z * s)

        # # TODO: Object Literals as StringMap?
        # # let literal = { x: 1, y: 2 }
        # # let doubled = functions.double(Vector(1, 2, 3))

        # let myLengthSquared = Vector(1, 2, 3).lengthSquared
        # let myScaled = Vector(1, 2, 3).scale(10)

        # let double = (a: Number) => a * 2
        let four = 2.triple.triple
        # how can we know that this is a reference to the triple function?
    "
